## Commits

### 00:02 — Narad [`52657d8`]
**feat: Phase 3 — Tapas self-evolution layer**

Buddha (DeepSeek V4 Pro) scores every avatar response after completion.
- score >= 0.75 → promoted to phase-3/sutras.jsonl
- score <  0.45 → flagged in weak_sessions.jsonl
- cosine similarity gate (0.92) deduplicates near-identical sutras
- sutra TTL default 90 days (tunable via TAPAS_SUTRA_TTL_DAYS)
- fire-and-forget: never blocks user response
- GET /sutras endpoint exposes live sutra bank stats

Co-Authored-By: Claude Sonnet 4.6 <noreply@anthropic.com>
